I'd like to offer some perspective to the common fan. You prob wonder how he can get up there and answer questions after losing? You prob feel bad for him ? One of the traits martial Arts gives to a human, is the ability to be humble. From the first day you walk into a gym, dojo, school, you are taught, losing is part of the bigger journey. If you lose and act like a bitch, you aren't evolving as a human. It's a perk of martial Arts training. Some of you can't believe he can cope with this loss. Some of you are in disbelief! I assure you now and forever, he's lost many many many times before and he has acquired the quality of humble within his soul.
